Root Route\n- **Route Path:** `/`\n- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/dashboard`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Notes:** Redirects to the Dashboard page.\n\n\n### 2. Dashboard Page\n- **Route Path:** `/dashboard`\n- **Function Name:** `dashboard`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured book data dictionaries.\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestseller books data dictionaries.\n- **Form Handling:** None (buttons navigate via GET requests).\n\n\n### 3. Book Catalog Page\n- **Route Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of books matching any search/filter criteria.\n  - `categories` (list of dict): List of category dictionaries for filter dropdown.\n  - `selected_category` (str): Currently selected category filter value.\n  - `search_query` (str): Current search input value.\n- **Form Handling:** Search and filter are handled as GET query parameters.\n\n\n### 4. Book Details Page\n- **Route Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `book_details`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict): Full detail of the selected book.\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews related to this book.\n- **Form Handling:** None on GET.\n\n- **Route Path (Add to Cart POST):** `/book/<int:book_id>/add_to_cart`\n- **Function Name:** `add_to_cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect back to the book details page.\n- **Form Handling:** Handles submission of add-to-cart action. Receives quantity (optional, assumed 1 if not specified).\n\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Route Path:** `/cart`\n- **Function Name:** `cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict includes cart item details such as book info and quantity.\n  - `total_amount` (float): Total price of all cart items.\n- **Form Handling:** None on GET.\n\n- **Route Path (Update Quantity POST):** `/cart/update_quantity/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `update_quantity`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles submission of updated quantity for a cart item.\n\n- **Route Path (Remove Item POST):** `/cart/remove_item/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `remove_item`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles removal of an item from the cart.\n\n- **Route Path (Proceed to Checkout GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n- **Route Path (POST place order):** `/checkout/place_order`\n- **Function Name:** `place_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/orders`\n- **Form Handling:** Receives customer name, shipping address, selected payment method. Processes order creation, clears cart.\n\n\n### 7. Order History Page\n- **Route Path:** `/orders`\n- **Function Name:** `order_history`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `orders.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict): List of orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.\n  - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).\n- **Form Handling:** Status filter applied via GET query parameter.\n\n- **Route Path (View Order Details GET):** `/orders/<int:order_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `view_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `order_details.html` (Assuming needed but user task does not specify page. Included for order detail view logic.)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `order` (dict): Details of the selected order.\n  - `order_items` (list of dict): List of items associated with order.\n- **Form Handling:** None\n\n\n### 8. Reviews Page\n- **Route Path:** `/reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews.\n  - `rating_filter` (str): Current rating filter (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).\n- **Form Handling:** Filter applied via GET query parameter.\n\n\n### 9. Write Review Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/write_review`\n- **Function Name:** `write_review_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of books eligible for review (typically purchased).\n\n- **Route Path (POST submit review):** `/write_review/submit`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/reviews`\n- **Form Handling:** Accepts book selection, rating (1-5), review text. Creates new review record.\n\n\n### 10. Bestsellers Page\n- **Route Path:** `/bestsellers`\n- **Function Name:** `bestsellers_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestsellers ranked with book info and sales count.\n  - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter (This Week, This Month, All Time).\n- **Form Handling:** Time period filter as GET query parameter.\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification\n\n### Template 1: Dashboard Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div) - Container for the dashboard page\n  - `featured-books` (Div) - Display featured book recommendations\n  - `browse-catalog-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/catalog`\n  - `view-cart-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/cart`\n  - `bestsellers-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/bestsellers`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict)\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `browse-catalog-button` -> url_for('book_catalog')\n  - `view-cart-button` -> url_for('cart')\n  - `bestsellers-button` -> url_for('bestsellers_page')\n\n\n### Template 2: Book Catalog Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/catalog.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Catalog\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Book Catalog\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `catalog-page` (Div) - Container for the catalog page\n  - `search-input` (Input) - Search field for filtering books by title, author, ISBN\n  - `category-filter` (Dropdown) - Filter dropdown for categories\n  - `books-grid` (Div) - Grid container for book cards\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button to view book details, one per book\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n  - `categories` (list of dict)\n  - `selected_category` (str)\n  - `search_query` (str)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` -> url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)\n\n\n### Template 3: Book Details Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/book_details.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Details\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Book Details\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `book-details-page` (Div) - Container for the page\n  - `book-title` (H1) - Displays book title\n  - `book-author` (Div) - Displays book author\n  - `book-price` (Div) - Displays book price\n  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button) - Button to add current book to cart\n  - `book-reviews` (Div) - Section displaying customer reviews\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form to `/book/<book_id>/add_to_cart`\n  - Quantity input hidden or fixed as 1 (not specified, assume 1)\n  - Submit button id: `add-to-cart-button`\n\n\n### Template 4: Shopping Cart Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/cart.html`\n- **Page Title:** Shopping Cart\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Shopping Cart\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `cart-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `cart-items-table` (Table) - Table listing cart items\n  - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number) - Input field for item quantity updates\n  - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) - Button to remove cart item\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button) - Button to navigate to checkout\n  - `total-amount` (Div) - Displays total cart amount\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict)\n  - `total_amount` (float)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` -> url_for('checkout')\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - Form(s) for quantity update and item removal each with POST method\n\n\n### Template 5: Checkout Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/checkout.html`\n- **Page Title:** Checkout\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Checkout\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `checkout-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `customer-name` (Input) - Customer name input field\n  - `shipping-address` (Textarea) - Shipping address input field\n  - `payment-method` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting payment method\n  - `place-order-button` (Button) - Submit button to place order\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form to `/checkout/place_order`\n  - Fields: customer-name, shipping-address, payment-method\n  - Submit button id: `place-order-button`\n\n\n### Template 6: Order History Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/orders.html`\n- **Page Title:** Order History\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Order History\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `orders-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `orders-table` (Table) - Displays orders list\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button) - Button to view order details\n  - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for status filtering\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict)\n  - `status_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` -> url_for('view_order', order_id=order_id)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> url_for('dashboard')\n\n\n### Template 7: Reviews Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/reviews.html`\n- **Page Title:** Customer Reviews\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Customer Reviews\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `reviews-list` (Div) - List of reviews\n  - `write-review-button` (Button) - Button to navigate to write review page\n  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n  - `rating_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `write-review-button` -> url_for('write_review_page')\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> url_for('dashboard')\n\n\n### Template 8: Write Review Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/write_review.html`\n- **Page Title:** Write a Review\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Write a Review\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `select-book` (Dropdown) - Book selection dropdown\n  - `rating-select` (Dropdown) - Rating selection dropdown (1-5 stars)\n  - `review-text` (Textarea) - Input area for review text\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button) - Submit button\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form to `/write_review/submit`\n  - Fields: select-book, rating-select, review-text\n  - Submit button id: `submit-review-button`\n\n\n### Template 9: Bestsellers Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/bestsellers.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bestsellers\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Bestsellers\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `bestsellers-page` (Div) - Container\n  - `bestsellers-list` (Div) - Ranked list of bestsellers\n  - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown) - Filter dropdown for time periods\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button to view book details per bestseller\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n  - `time_period` (str)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` -> url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> url_for('dashboard')\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification\n\n### 1. Books Data\n- **File Path:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `category` (str)\n  6. `price` (float)\n  7. `stock` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores all book information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel\n  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind\n  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction\n  ```\n\n\n### 2. Categories Data\n- **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `category_id` (int)\n  2. `category_name` (str)\n  3. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores book category information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels\n  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books\n  3|Science|Scientific topics and research\n  ```\n\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File Path:** `data/cart.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `cart_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `quantity` (int)\n  4. `added_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n- **Description:** Stores shopping cart items.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File Path:** `data/orders.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_id` (int)\n  2. `customer_name` (str)\n  3. `order_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n  4. `total_amount` (float)\n  5. `status` (str)\n  6. `shipping_address` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores customer orders with tracking status.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001\n  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001\n  ```\n\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File Path:** `data/order_items.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_item_id` (int)\n  2. `order_id` (int)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `quantity` (int)\n  5. `price` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores individual items within each order.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|3|1|14.99\n  3|2|2|1|16.99\n  ```\n\n\n### 6. Reviews Data\n- **File Path:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `customer_name` (str)\n  4. `rating` (int, 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n- **Description:** Stores customer reviews for books.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n\n### 7. Bestsellers Data\n- **File Path:** `data/bestsellers.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `sales_count` (int)\n  3. `period` (str) - Time period (e.g., This Week, This Month, All Time)\n- **Description:** Stores bestseller rankings by sales count and period.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  2|150|This Month\n  1|120|This Month\n  3|95|This Month\n  ```\n\n---\n\n**End of Design Specification Document**\n",

        "before": "# BookstoreOnline - Design Specification Document\n\n---\n\n## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification\n\n### 1. Root Route\n- **Route Path:** `/`\n- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/dashboard`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Notes:** Redirects to the Dashboard page.\n\n\n### 2. Dashboard Page\n- **Route Path:** `/dashboard`\n- **Function Name:** `dashboard`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured book data dictionaries.\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestseller books data dictionaries.\n- **Form Handling:** None (buttons navigate via GET requests).\n\n\n### 3. Book Catalog Page\n- **Route Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of books matching any search/filter criteria.\n  - `categories` (list of dict): List of category dictionaries for filter dropdown.\n  - `selected_category` (str): Currently selected category filter value.\n  - `search_query` (str): Current search input value.\n- **Form Handling:** Search and filter are handled as GET query parameters.\n\n\n### 4. Book Details Page\n- **Route Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `book_details`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict): Full detail of the selected book.\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews related to this book.\n- **Form Handling:** None on GET.\n\n- **Route Path (Add to Cart POST):** `/book/<int:book_id>/add_to_cart`\n- **Function Name:** `add_to_cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect back to the book details page.\n- **Form Handling:** Handles submission of add-to-cart action. Receives quantity (optional, assumed 1 if not specified).\n\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Route Path:** `/cart`\n- **Function Name:** `cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict includes cart item details such as book info and quantity.\n  - `total_amount` (float): Total price of all cart items.\n- **Form Handling:** None on GET.\n\n- **Route Path (Update Quantity POST):** `/cart/update_quantity/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `update_quantity`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles submission of updated quantity for a cart item.\n\n- **Route Path (Remove Item POST):** `/cart/remove_item/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `remove_item`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles removal of an item from the cart.\n\n- **Route Path (Proceed to Checkout GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n- **Route Path (POST place order):** `/checkout/place_order`\n- **Function Name:** `place_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/orders`\n- **Form Handling:** Receives customer name, shipping address, selected payment method. Processes order creation, clears cart.\n\n\n### 7. Order History Page\n- **Route Path:** `/orders`\n- **Function Name:** `order_history`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `orders.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict): List of orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.\n  - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).\n- **Form Handling:** Status filter applied via GET query parameter.\n\n- **Route Path (View Order Details GET):** `/orders/<int:order_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `view_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `order_details.html` (Assuming needed but user task does not specify page. Included for order detail view logic.)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `order` (dict): Details of the selected order.\n  - `order_items` (list of dict): List of items associated with order.\n- **Form Handling:** None\n\n\n### 8. Reviews Page\n- **Route Path:** `/reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews.\n  - `rating_filter` (str): Current rating filter (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).\n- **Form Handling:** Filter applied via GET query parameter.\n\n\n### 9. Write Review Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/write_review`\n- **Function Name:** `write_review_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of books eligible for review (typically purchased).\n\n- **Route Path (POST submit review):** `/write_review/submit`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/reviews`\n- **Form Handling:** Accepts book selection, rating (1-5), review text. Creates new review record.\n\n\n### 10. Bestsellers Page\n- **Route Path:** `/bestsellers`\n- **Function Name:** `bestsellers_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestsellers ranked with book info and sales count.\n  - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter (This Week, This Month, All Time).\n- **Form Handling:** Time period filter as GET query parameter.\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification\n\n### Template 1: Dashboard Page\n- **File Path:** `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Main H1 Heading:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - Books Data\n- **File Path:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `category` (str)\n  6. `price` (float)\n  7. `stock` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores all book information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel\n  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind\n  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction\n  ```\n\n\n### 2. Categories Data\n- **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `category_id` (int)\n  2. `category_name` (str)\n  3. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores book category information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels\n  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books\n  3|Science|Scientific topics and research\n  ```\n\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File Path:** `data/cart.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `cart_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `quantity` (int)\n  4. `added_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n- **Description:** Stores shopping cart items.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File Path:** `data/orders.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_id` (int)\n  2. `customer_name` (str)\n  3. `order_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n  4. `total_amount` (float)\n  5. `status` (str)\n  6. `shipping_address` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores customer orders with tracking status.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001\n  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001\n  ```\n\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File Path:** `data/order_items.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_item_id` (int)\n  2. `order_id` (int)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `quantity` (int)\n  5. `price` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores individual items within each order.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|3|1|14.99\n  3|2|2|1|16.99\n  ```\n\n\n### 6. Reviews Data\n- **File Path:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `customer_name` (str)\n  4. `rating` (int, 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)\n- **Description:** Stores customer reviews for books.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n\n### 7. Bestsellers Data\n- **File Path:** `data/bestsellers.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `sales_count` (int)\n  3. `period` (str) - Time period (e.g., This Week, This Month, All Time)\n- **Description:** Stores bestseller rankings by sales count and period.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  2|150|This Month\n  1|120|This Month\n  3|95|This Month\n  ```\n\n---\n\n**End of Design Specification Document**\n",

Root Route\n- **Route Path:** `/`\n- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/dashboard`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Description:** Redirects the user to the Dashboard page.\n\n\n### 2. Dashboard Page\n- **Route Path:** `/dashboard`\n- **Function Name:** `dashboard`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured book data dictionaries.\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestseller books data dictionaries.\n\n\n### 3. Book Catalog Page\n- **Route Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of available books filtered by search and category.\n  - `categories` (list of dict): List of categories for filtering.\n  - `selected_category` (str): The category filter selected by the user.\n  - `search_query` (str): Search string entered by the user.\n\n\n### 4. Book Details Page\n- **Route Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `book_details`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict): Detailed information of the selected book.\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): Customer reviews for the book.\n\n- **Route Path (Add To Cart POST):** `/book/<int:book_id>/add_to_cart`\n- **Function Name:** `add_to_cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles adding the selected book to the shopping cart. Quantity assumed to be 1 by default.\n\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Route Path:** `/cart`\n- **Function Name:** `cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Items currently in the shopping cart.\n  - `total_amount` (float): Total cost of all items in the cart.\n\n- **Route Path (Update Quantity POST):** `/cart/update_quantity/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `update_quantity`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Updates the quantity for a specific cart item.\n\n- **Route Path (Remove Item POST):** `/cart/remove_item/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `remove_item`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Removes an item from the cart.\n\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n- **Route Path (POST - Place Order):** `/checkout/place_order`\n- **Function Name:** `place_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/orders`\n- **Form Handling:** Processes the checkout form, creates order record, clears the cart.\n\n\n### 7. Order History Page\n- **Route Path:** `/orders`\n- **Function Name:** `order_history`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `orders.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict): List of user orders with ID, date, total, and status.\n  - `status_filter` (str): The status filter applied (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).\n\n- **Route Path (View Order Details GET):** `/orders/<int:order_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `view_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** *Note: Order detail page not specified in user task, implementation optional.*\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `order` (dict): Selected order details.\n  - `order_items` (list of dict): Items in the selected order.\n\n\n### 8. Reviews Page\n- **Route Path:** `/reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of customer reviews.\n  - `rating_filter` (str): Current rating filter applied.\n\n\n### 9. Write Review Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/write_review`\n- **Function Name:** `write_review_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): Books eligible for review.\n\n- **Route Path (POST):** `/write_review/submit`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/reviews`\n- **Form Handling:** Processes review submission form fields: book selected, rating, and review text.\n\n\n### 10. Bestsellers Page\n- **Route Path:** `/bestsellers`\n- **Function Name:** `bestsellers_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Ranked list of bestselling books.\n  - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter (This Week, This Month, All Time).\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification\n\n### Template 1: Dashboard Page\n- **File:** `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div) - Container for entire dashboard page.\n  - `featured-books` (Div) - Displays featured book recommendations.\n  - `browse-catalog-button` (Button) - Navigates to Catalog page.\n  - `view-cart-button` (Button) - Navigates to Shopping Cart page.\n  - `bestsellers-button` (Button) - Navigates to Bestsellers page.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict)\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - Buttons use `url_for`:\n    - `browse-catalog-button` -> `url_for('book_catalog')`\n    - `view-cart-button` -> `url_for('cart')`\n    - `bestsellers-button` -> `url_for('bestsellers_page')`\n\n\n### Template 2: Book Catalog Page\n- **File:** `templates/catalog.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Catalog\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Book Catalog\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `catalog-page` (Div) - Container for catalog page.\n  - `search-input` (Input) - Search field to enter query by title, author, ISBN.\n  - `category-filter` (Dropdown) - Select book category filter.\n  - `books-grid` (Div) - Grid to display books as cards.\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button on each book card to view details.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n  - `categories` (list of dict)\n  - `selected_category` (str)\n  - `search_query` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` button links to `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`\n\n\n### Template 3: Book Details Page\n- **File:** `templates/book_details.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Details\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Book Details\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `book-details-page` (Div) - Container for book details page.\n  - `book-title` (H1) - Displays the book title.\n  - `book-author` (Div) - Displays the book author.\n  - `book-price` (Div) - Displays book price.\n  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button) - Button to add book to cart.\n  - `book-reviews` (Div) - Shows customer reviews for the book.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form targeting `/book/<book_id>/add_to_cart`\n  - Includes submit button with ID `add-to-cart-button`\n  - Quantity input is assumed fixed at 1 (not specified otherwise)\n\n\n### Template 4: Shopping Cart Page\n- **File:** `templates/cart.html`\n- **Page Title:** Shopping Cart\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Shopping Cart\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `cart-page` (Div) - Container for cart page.\n  - `cart-items-table` (Table) - Lists cart items with columns: title, quantity, price, subtotal.\n  - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input, number) - Input for updating quantity per item.\n  - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) - Button to remove item from cart.\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button) - Button to proceed to checkout.\n  - `total-amount` (Div) - Displays total cart amount.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict)\n  - `total_amount` (float)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` -> `url_for('checkout')`\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST forms for update quantity and remove item actions.\n\n\n### Template 5: Checkout Page\n- **File:** `templates/checkout.html`\n- **Page Title:** Checkout\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Checkout\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `checkout-page` (Div) - Container for checkout page.\n  - `customer-name` (Input) - Field for entering customer name.\n  - `shipping-address` (Textarea) - Field for entering shipping address.\n  - `payment-method` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).\n  - `place-order-button` (Button) - Button to submit order form.\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form submitting to `/checkout/place_order`\n  - Fields: `customer-name`, `shipping-address`, `payment-method`\n  - Submit button ID: `place-order-button`\n\n\n### Template 6: Order History Page\n- **File:** `templates/orders.html`\n- **Page Title:** Order History\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Order History\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `orders-page` (Div) - Container for orders page.\n  - `orders-table` (Table) - Displays orders with columns: order ID, date, total amount, status.\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button) - Button to view details of an order.\n  - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter orders by status.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict)\n  - `status_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` -> `url_for('view_order', order_id=order_id)`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n\n### Template 7: Reviews Page\n- **File:** `templates/reviews.html`\n- **Page Title:** Customer Reviews\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Customer Reviews\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `reviews-page` (Div) - Container for reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` (Div) - Displays all reviews including book title, rating, review text.\n  - `write-review-button` (Button) - Button navigating to write review page.\n  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n  - `rating_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `write-review-button` -> `url_for('write_review_page')`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n\n### Template 8: Write Review Page\n- **File:** `templates/write_review.html`\n- **Page Title:** Write a Review\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Write a Review\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `write-review-page` (Div) - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-book` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to select book to review.\n  - `rating-select` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting rating (1-5 stars).\n  - `review-text` (Textarea) - Textarea to write review.\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button) - Button to submit review form.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form to `/write_review/submit`\n  - Fields: `select-book`, `rating-select`, `review-text`\n  - Submit button ID: `submit-review-button`\n\n\n### Template 9: Bestsellers Page\n- **File:** `templates/bestsellers.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bestsellers\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Bestsellers\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `bestsellers-page` (Div) - Container for bestsellers page.\n  - `bestsellers-list` (Div) - Displays ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, sales count.\n  - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter by time period.\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button on each bestseller item to view details.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n  - `time_period` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` -> `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification\n\n### 1. Books Data\n- **File:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `category` (str)\n  6. `price` (float)\n  7. `stock` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores all book records with details.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel\n  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind\n  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction\n  ```\n\n\n### 2. Categories Data\n- **File:** `data/categories.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `category_id` (int)\n  2. `category_name` (str)\n  3. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores categories of books with descriptions.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels\n  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books\n  3|Science|Scientific topics and research\n  ```\n\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File:** `data/cart.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `cart_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `quantity` (int)\n  4. `added_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n- **Description:** Stores shopping cart items and quantity.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File:** `data/orders.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_id` (int)\n  2. `customer_name` (str)\n  3. `order_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n  4. `total_amount` (float)\n  5. `status` (str)\n  6. `shipping_address` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores orders placed by customers.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001\n  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001\n  ```\n\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File:** `data/order_items.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_item_id` (int)\n  2. `order_id` (int)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `quantity` (int)\n  5. `price` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores items associated with each order.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|3|1|14.99\n  3|2|2|1|16.99\n  ```\n\n\n### 6. Reviews Data\n- **File:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `customer_name` (str)\n  4. `rating` (int, 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n- **Description:** Stores customer reviews for books.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n\n### 7. Bestsellers Data\n- **File:** `data/bestsellers.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `sales_count` (int)\n  3. `period` (str) - Example values: This Week, This Month, All Time\n- **Description:** Stores bestsellers ranking data per time period.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  2|150|This Month\n  1|120|This Month\n  3|95|This Month\n  ```\n\n---\n\n**End of Design Specification Document**\n",

        "before": "# BookstoreOnline - Design Specification Document\n\n---\n\n## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification\n\n### 1. Root Route\n- **Route Path:** `/`\n- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/dashboard`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Description:** Redirects the user to the Dashboard page.\n\n\n### 2. Dashboard Page\n- **Route Path:** `/dashboard`\n- **Function Name:** `dashboard`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured book data dictionaries.\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestseller books data dictionaries.\n\n\n### 3. Book Catalog Page\n- **Route Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of available books filtered by search and category.\n  - `categories` (list of dict): List of categories for filtering.\n  - `selected_category` (str): The category filter selected by the user.\n  - `search_query` (str): Search string entered by the user.\n\n\n### 4. Book Details Page\n- **Route Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `book_details`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict): Detailed information of the selected book.\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): Customer reviews for the book.\n\n- **Route Path (Add To Cart POST):** `/book/<int:book_id>/add_to_cart`\n- **Function Name:** `add_to_cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Form Handling:** Handles adding the selected book to the shopping cart. Quantity assumed to be 1 by default.\n\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Route Path:** `/cart`\n- **Function Name:** `cart`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict): Items currently in the shopping cart.\n  - `total_amount` (float): Total cost of all items in the cart.\n\n- **Route Path (Update Quantity POST):** `/cart/update_quantity/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `update_quantity`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Updates the quantity for a specific cart item.\n\n- **Route Path (Remove Item POST):** `/cart/remove_item/<int:item_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `remove_item`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`\n- **Form Handling:** Removes an item from the cart.\n\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/checkout`\n- **Function Name:** `checkout`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`\n- **Context Variables:** None\n\n- **Route Path (POST - Place Order):** `/checkout/place_order`\n- **Function Name:** `place_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/orders`\n- **Form Handling:** Processes the checkout form, creates order record, clears the cart.\n\n\n### 7. Order History Page\n- **Route Path:** `/orders`\n- **Function Name:** `order_history`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `orders.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict): List of user orders with ID, date, total, and status.\n  - `status_filter` (str): The status filter applied (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).\n\n- **Route Path (View Order Details GET):** `/orders/<int:order_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `view_order`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** *Note: Order detail page not specified in user task, implementation optional.*\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `order` (dict): Selected order details.\n  - `order_items` (list of dict): Items in the selected order.\n\n\n### 8. Reviews Page\n- **Route Path:** `/reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of customer reviews.\n  - `rating_filter` (str): Current rating filter applied.\n\n\n### 9. Write Review Page\n- **Route Path (GET):** `/write_review`\n- **Function Name:** `write_review_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict): Books eligible for review.\n\n- **Route Path (POST):** `/write_review/submit`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/reviews`\n- **Form Handling:** Processes review submission form fields: book selected, rating, and review text.\n\n\n### 10. Bestsellers Page\n- **Route Path:** `/bestsellers`\n- **Function Name:** `bestsellers_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict): Ranked list of bestselling books.\n  - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter (This Week, This Month, All Time).\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification\n\n### Template 1: Dashboard Page\n- **File:** `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Bookstore Dashboard\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div) - Container for entire dashboard page.\n  - `featured-books` (Div) - Displays featured book recommendations.\n  - `browse-catalog-button` (Button) - Navigates to Catalog page.\n  - `view-cart-button` (Button) - Navigates to Shopping Cart page.\n  - `bestsellers-button` (Button) - Navigates to Bestsellers page.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict)\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - Buttons use `url_for`:\n    - `browse-catalog-button` -> `url_for('book_catalog')`\n    - `view-cart-button` -> `url_for('cart')`\n    - `bestsellers-button` -> `url_for('bestsellers_page')`\n\n\n### Template 2: Book Catalog Page\n- **File:** `templates/catalog.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Catalog\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Book Catalog\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `catalog-page` (Div) - Container for catalog page.\n  - `search-input` (Input) - Search field to enter query by title, author, ISBN.\n  - `category-filter` (Dropdown) - Select book category filter.\n  - `books-grid` (Div) - Grid to display books as cards.\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button on each book card to view details.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n  - `categories` (list of dict)\n  - `selected_category` (str)\n  - `search_query` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` button links to `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`\n\n\n### Template 3: Book Details Page\n- **File:** `templates/book_details.html`\n- **Page Title:** Book Details\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Book Details\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `book-details-page` (Div) - Container for book details page.\n  - `book-title` (H1) - Displays the book title.\n  - `book-author` (Div) - Displays the book author.\n  - `book-price` (Div) - Displays book price.\n  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button) - Button to add book to cart.\n  - `book-reviews` (Div) - Shows customer reviews for the book.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form targeting `/book/<book_id>/add_to_cart`\n  - Includes submit button with ID `add-to-cart-button`\n  - Quantity input is assumed fixed at 1 (not specified otherwise)\n\n\n### Template 4: Shopping Cart Page\n- **File:** `templates/cart.html`\n- **Page Title:** Shopping Cart\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Shopping Cart\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `cart-page` (Div) - Container for cart page.\n  - `cart-items-table` (Table) - Lists cart items with columns: title, quantity, price, subtotal.\n  - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input, number) - Input for updating quantity per item.\n  - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) - Button to remove item from cart.\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button) - Button to proceed to checkout.\n  - `total-amount` (Div) - Displays total cart amount.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `cart_items` (list of dict)\n  - `total_amount` (float)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` -> `url_for('checkout')`\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST forms for update quantity and remove item actions.\n\n\n### Template 5: Checkout Page\n- **File:** `templates/checkout.html`\n- **Page Title:** Checkout\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Checkout\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `checkout-page` (Div) - Container for checkout page.\n  - `customer-name` (Input) - Field for entering customer name.\n  - `shipping-address` (Textarea) - Field for entering shipping address.\n  - `payment-method` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).\n  - `place-order-button` (Button) - Button to submit order form.\n- **Context Variables:** None\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form submitting to `/checkout/place_order`\n  - Fields: `customer-name`, `shipping-address`, `payment-method`\n  - Submit button ID: `place-order-button`\n\n\n### Template 6: Order History Page\n- **File:** `templates/orders.html`\n- **Page Title:** Order History\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Order History\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `orders-page` (Div) - Container for orders page.\n  - `orders-table` (Table) - Displays orders with columns: order ID, date, total amount, status.\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` (Button) - Button to view details of an order.\n  - `order-status-filter` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter orders by status.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `orders` (list of dict)\n  - `status_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-order-button-{order_id}` -> `url_for('view_order', order_id=order_id)`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n\n### Template 7: Reviews Page\n- **File:** `templates/reviews.html`\n- **Page Title:** Customer Reviews\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Customer Reviews\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `reviews-page` (Div) - Container for reviews page.\n  - `reviews-list` (Div) - Displays all reviews including book title, rating, review text.\n  - `write-review-button` (Button) - Button navigating to write review page.\n  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n  - `rating_filter` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `write-review-button` -> `url_for('write_review_page')`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n\n### Template 8: Write Review Page\n- **File:** `templates/write_review.html`\n- **Page Title:** Write a Review\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Write a Review\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `write-review-page` (Div) - Container for write review page.\n  - `select-book` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to select book to review.\n  - `rating-select` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting rating (1-5 stars).\n  - `review-text` (Textarea) - Textarea to write review.\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button) - Button to submit review form.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` (list of dict)\n- **Form Structure:**\n  - POST form to `/write_review/submit`\n  - Fields: `select-book`, `rating-select`, `review-text`\n  - Submit button ID: `submit-review-button`\n\n\n### Template 9: Bestsellers Page\n- **File:** `templates/bestsellers.html`\n- **Page Title:** Bestsellers\n- **Main <h1> Heading:** Bestsellers\n- **Element IDs and Purpose:**\n  - `bestsellers-page` (Div) - Container for bestsellers page.\n  - `bestsellers-list` (Div) - Displays ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, sales count.\n  - `time-period-filter` (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter by time period.\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button on each bestseller item to view details.\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) - Button to return to dashboard.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bestsellers` (list of dict)\n  - `time_period` (str)\n- **Navigation:**\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` -> `url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification\n\n### 1. Books Data\n- **File:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `category` (str)\n  6. `price` (float)\n  7. `stock` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores all book records with details.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel\n  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind\n  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction\n  ```\n\n\n### 2. Categories Data\n- **File:** `data/categories.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `category_id` (int)\n  2. `category_name` (str)\n  3. `description` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores categories of books with descriptions.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels\n  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books\n  3|Science|Scientific topics and research\n  ```\n\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File:** `data/cart.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `cart_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `quantity` (int)\n  4. `added_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n- **Description:** Stores shopping cart items and quantity.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File:** `data/orders.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_id` (int)\n  2. `customer_name` (str)\n  3. `order_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n  4. `total_amount` (float)\n  5. `status` (str)\n  6. `shipping_address` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores orders placed by customers.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001\n  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001\n  ```\n\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File:** `data/order_items.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `order_item_id` (int)\n  2. `order_id` (int)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `quantity` (int)\n  5. `price` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores items associated with each order.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|3|1|14.99\n  3|2|2|1|16.99\n  ```\n\n\n### 6. Reviews Data\n- **File:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `book_id` (int)\n  3. `customer_name` (str)\n  4. `rating` (int, 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, yyyy-mm-dd)\n- **Description:** Stores customer reviews for books.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n\n### 7. Bestsellers Data\n- **File:** `data/bestsellers.txt`\n- **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)\n- **Fields Order:**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `sales_count` (int)\n  3. `period` (str) - Example values: This Week, This Month, All Time\n- **Description:** Stores bestsellers ranking data per time period.\n- **Example Data:**\n  ```\n  2|150|This Month\n  1|120|This Month\n  3|95|This Month\n  ```\n\n---\n\n**End of Design Specification Document**\n",

         # BookstoreOnline - Design Specification Document
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - **Route Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/dashboard`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         - **Notes:** Redirects to the Dashboard page.
         
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - **Route Path:** `/dashboard`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured book data dictionaries.
           - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestseller books data dictionaries.
         - **Form Handling:** None (buttons navigate via GET requests).
         
         
         ### 3. Book Catalog Page
         - **Route Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `book_catalog`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` (list of dict): List of books matching any search/filter criteria.
           - `categories` (list of dict): List of category dictionaries for filter dropdown.
           - `selected_category` (str): Currently selected category filter value.
           - `search_query` (str): Current search input value.
         - **Form Handling:** Search and filter are handled as GET query parameters.
         
         
         ### 4. Book Details Page
         - **Route Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `book_details`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book` (dict): Full detail of the selected book.
           - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews related to this book.
         - **Form Handling:** None on GET.
         
         - **Route Path (Add to Cart POST):** `/book/<int:book_id>/add_to_cart`
         - **Function Name:** `add_to_cart`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect back to the book details page.
         - **Form Handling:** Handles submission of add-to-cart action. Receives quantity (optional, assumed 1 if not specified).
         
         
         ### 5. Shopping Cart Page
         - **Route Path:** `/cart`
         - **Function Name:** `cart`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `cart.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `cart_items` (list of dict): Each dict includes cart item details such as book info and quantity.
           - `total_amount` (float): Total price of all cart items.
         - **Form Handling:** None on GET.
         
         - **Route Path (Update Quantity POST):** `/cart/update_quantity/<int:item_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `update_quantity`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`
         - **Form Handling:** Handles submission of updated quantity for a cart item.
         
         - **Route Path (Remove Item POST):** `/cart/remove_item/<int:item_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `remove_item`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/cart`
         - **Form Handling:** Handles removal of an item from the cart.
         
         - **Route Path (Proceed to Checkout GET):** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         
         
         ### 6. Checkout Page
         - **Route Path (GET):** `/checkout`
         - **Function Name:** `checkout`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `checkout.html`
         - **Context Variables:** None
         
         - **Route Path (POST place order):** `/checkout/place_order`
         - **Function Name:** `place_order`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/orders`
         - **Form Handling:** Receives customer name, shipping address, selected payment method. Processes order creation, clears cart.
         
         
         ### 7. Order History Page
         - **Route Path:** `/orders`
         - **Function Name:** `order_history`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `orders.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `orders` (list of dict): List of orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.
           - `status_filter` (str): Current status filter (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
         - **Form Handling:** Status filter applied via GET query parameter.
         
         - **Route Path (View Order Details GET):** `/orders/<int:order_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `view_order`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `order_details.html` (Assuming needed but user task does not specify page. Included for order detail view logic.)
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `order` (dict): Details of the selected order.
           - `order_items` (list of dict): List of items associated with order.
         - **Form Handling:** None
         
         
         ### 8. Reviews Page
         - **Route Path:** `/reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `reviews_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews.
           - `rating_filter` (str): Current rating filter (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).
         - **Form Handling:** Filter applied via GET query parameter.
         
         
         ### 9. Write Review Page
         - **Route Path (GET):** `/write_review`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` (list of dict): List of books eligible for review (typically purchased).
         
         - **Route Path (POST submit review):** `/write_review/submit`
         - **Function Name:** `submit_review`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Redirect to `/reviews`
         - **Form Handling:** Accepts book selection, rating (1-5), review text. Creates new review record.
         
         
         ### 10. Bestsellers Page
         - **Route Path:** `/bestsellers`
         - **Function Name:** `bestsellers_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `bestsellers.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `bestsellers` (list of dict): List of bestsellers ranked with book info and sales count.
           - `time_period` (str): Selected time period filter (This Week, This Month, All Time).
         - **Form Handling:** Time period filter as GET query parameter.
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### Template 1: Dashboard Page
         - **File Path:** `templates/dashboard.html`
         - **Page Title:** Bookstore Dashboard
         - **Main H1 Heading:** Bookstore Dashboard
         - **Element IDs:**
           - `dashboard-page` (Div) - Container for the dashboard page
           - `featured-books` (Div) - Display featured book recommendations
           - `browse-catalog-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/catalog`
           - `view-cart-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/cart`
           - `bestsellers-button` (Button) - Navigates to `/bestsellers`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `featured_books` (list of dict)
           - `bestsellers` (list of dict)
         - **Navigation Mappings:**
           - `browse-catalog-button` -> url_for('book_catalog')
           - `view-cart-button` -> url_for('cart')
           - `bestsellers-button` -> url_for('bestsellers_page')
         
         
         ### Template 2: Book Catalog Page
         - **File Path:** `templates/catalog.html`
         - **Page Title:** Book Catalog
         - **Main H1 Heading:** Book Catalog
         - **Element IDs:**
           - `catalog-page` (Div) - Container for the catalog page
           - `search-input` (Input) - Search field for filtering books by title, author, ISBN
           - `category-filter` (Dropdown) - Filter dropdown for categories
           - `books-grid` (Div) - Grid container for book cards
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - Button to view book details, one per book
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` (list of dict)
           - `categories` (list of dict)
           - `selected_category` (str)
           - `search_query` (str)
         - **Navigation Mappings:**
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` -> url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id)
         
         
         ### Template 3: Book Details Page
         - **File Path:** `templates/book_details.html`
         - **Page Title:** Book Details
         - **Main H1 Heading:** Book Details
         - **Element IDs:**
           - `book-details-page` (Div) - Container for the page
           - `book-title` (H1) - Displays book title
           - `book-author` (Div) - Displays book author

         - **Context Variables:**

           - `reviews` (list of dict)
         - **Form Structure:**

           - Quantity input hidden or fixed as 1 (not specified, assume 1)
           - Submit button id: `add-to-cart-button`
         
         
         ### Template 4: Shopping Cart Page
         - **File Path:** `templates/cart.html`

           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button) - Button to remove cart item
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button) - Button to navigate to checkout
           - `total-amount` (Div) - Displays total cart amount
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `cart_items` (list of dict)
           - `total_amount` (float)
         - **Navigation Mappings:**
           - `proceed-checkout-button` -> url_for('checkout')
         - **Form Structure:**
           - Form(s) for quantity update and item removal each with POST method
         
         
         ### Template 5: Checkout Page
         - **File Path:** `templates/checkout.html`
         - **Page Title:** Checkout
         - **Main H1 Heading:** Checkout
         - **Element IDs:**
           - `checkout-page` (Div) - Container

           - `shipping-address` (Textarea) - Shipping address input field
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown) - Dropdown for selecting payment method

         - **Form Structure:**

         ## Section 3: Data Schemas Specification
         
         ### 1. Books Data
         - **File Path:** `data/books.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `category` (str)
           6. `price` (float)
           7. `stock` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Stores all book information.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
           2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
           3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
           ```
         
         
         ### 2. Categories Data
         - **File Path:** `data/categories.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `category_id` (int)
           2. `category_name` (str)
           3. `description` (str)
         - **Description:** Stores book category information.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
           2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
           3|Science|Scientific topics and research
           ```
         
         
         ### 3. Cart Data
         - **File Path:** `data/cart.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `cart_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `quantity` (int)
           4. `added_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Description:** Stores shopping cart items.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         
         ### 4. Orders Data
         - **File Path:** `data/orders.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `order_id` (int)
           2. `customer_name` (str)
           3. `order_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)
           4. `total_amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str)
           6. `shipping_address` (str)
         - **Description:** Stores customer orders with tracking status.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
           2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
           ```
         
         
         ### 5. Order Items Data
         - **File Path:** `data/order_items.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `order_item_id` (int)
           2. `order_id` (int)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `quantity` (int)
           5. `price` (float)
         - **Description:** Stores individual items within each order.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|3|1|14.99
           3|2|2|1|16.99
           ```
         
         
         ### 6. Reviews Data
         - **File Path:** `data/reviews.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `book_id` (int)
           3. `customer_name` (str)
           4. `rating` (int, 1-5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (str, format `YYYY-MM-DD`)
         - **Description:** Stores customer reviews for books.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
           3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
           ```
         
         
         ### 7. Bestsellers Data
         - **File Path:** `data/bestsellers.txt`
         - **Format:** Pipe-delimited (`|`)
         - **Fields Order:**
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `sales_count` (int)
           3. `period` (str) - Time period (e.g., This Week, This Month, All Time)
         - **Description:** Stores bestseller rankings by sales count and period.
         - **Example Rows:**
           ```
           2|150|This Month
           1|120|This Month
           3|95|This Month
           ```
         
         ---
         
         **End of Design Specification Document**
